namespace = giga_psychic_beacon

# Activate beacon
country_event = {
	id = giga_psychic_beacon.001
	title = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.name"
	desc = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal

	diplomatic = yes

	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = shroud1
		room = shroud_room
	}

	option = { # Illuminate (Change planet class from shrouded to lifeless)
		name = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.a"
		custom_tooltip = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.a.tooltip"
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_psionic_sublimate value >= 20 }
			custom_tooltip = {
				fail_text = "can_already_illuminate"
				NOT = { has_country_flag = giga_psychic_beacon_illumiate }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				fail_text = "must_have_shrouded_world"
				any_planet_within_border = { 
					OR = {
						is_planet_class = pc_shrouded
						has_modifier = beacon_shrouded_habitable_structure
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_resource = { sr_psionic_sublimate = -20 }
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = giga_psychic_beacon_illumiate }
	}

	option = { # Traverse (+1000% jumpdrive range)
		name = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.b"
		custom_tooltip = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.b.tooltip"
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_psionic_sublimate value >= 30 }
			NOT = { has_modifier = "giga_psychic_traverse" }
		}
		add_resource = { sr_psionic_sublimate = -50 }
		add_modifier = { modifier = "giga_psychic_traverse" days = 900 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = giga_psychic_beacon.009 } }
	}

	option = { # Dominate (Convert pops on hostile planets to psionic)
		name = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.c"
		custom_tooltip = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.c.tooltip"
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_psionic_sublimate value >= 200 }
			custom_tooltip = {
				fail_text = "must_be_at_war_and_own_systems"
				any_country = {
					is_at_war_with = root
					OR = {
						ehof_default_country = yes
						is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
					}
					any_planet_within_border = {
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = ROOT
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_resource = { sr_psionic_sublimate = -200 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = giga_psychic_beacon.003 } }
	}

	option = { # Imprison (Any hostile colony > shrouded world)
		name = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.d"
		custom_tooltip = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.d.tooltip"
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_psionic_sublimate value >= 1000 }
			custom_tooltip = {
				fail_text = "must_be_at_war"
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_at_war_with = root
						OR = {
							ehof_default_country = yes
							is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
						}				
					}
					any_country = {
						has_country_flag = paluush_primitives
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_resource = { sr_psionic_sublimate = -1000 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = giga_psychic_beacon.005 } }
	}

	option = { # Conjure (Spawn psionic armies on enemy world)
		name = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.e"
		custom_tooltip = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.e.tooltip"
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_psionic_sublimate value >= 60 }
			custom_tooltip = {
				fail_text = "must_be_at_war"
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_at_war_with = root
						OR = {
							ehof_default_country = yes
							is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium
						}				
					}
					any_country = {
						has_country_flag = paluush_primitives
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_resource = { sr_psionic_sublimate = -60 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = giga_psychic_beacon.010 } }
	}

	option = { # Imprint (Buff admiral)
		name = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.f"
		custom_tooltip = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.f.tooltip"
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_psionic_sublimate value >= 100 }
			custom_tooltip = {
				fail_text = "must_have_valid_beacon_admiral"
				any_owned_leader = {
					leader_class = admiral
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							has_trait = leader_trait_admiral_astute
							has_trait = leader_trait_admiral_farsighted
							has_trait = leader_trait_admiral_fortifier
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_resource = { sr_psionic_sublimate = -100 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = giga_psychic_beacon.015 } }
	}

	option = { # Exit
		default_hide_option = yes
		name = "giga_psychic_beacon.001.g"
	}

	after = {
		random_owned_megastructure = {
			limit = { is_megastructure_type = psychic_beacon_4 }
			solar_system = { spawn_megastructure = { type = "psychic_beacon_3" location = prev.planet owner = root } }
			remove_megastructure = this
		}
	}
}

# Planet Illuminated
country_event = {
	id = giga_psychic_beacon.002
	title = "giga_psychic_beacon.002.name"
	desc = "giga_psychic_beacon.002.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_zro_3
	location = event_target:giga_planet_illuminated
	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	option = { name = "giga_psychic_beacon.002.a" }
}

# Ezics mutate
country_event = {
	id = giga_psychic_beacon.00611
	title = "giga_psychic_beacon.00611.name"
	desc = "giga_psychic_beacon.00611.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_zro_1
	location = event_target:gigaflusion
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		event_target:gigaflusion = {
			create_species = {
				name = "Infused Ezicania"
				plural = "Infused Ezicanias"
				class = REP
				portrait = rep10
				homeworld = event_target:gigaflusion
				traits = {
					trait = trait_pc_ocean_preference
					trait = trait_venerable
					trait = trait_adaptive
					trait = trait_quick_learners
					trait = trait_strong
					trait = trait_talented
					trait = trait_robust
					trait = trait_psionic
				}
				effect = {
					save_global_event_target_as = infusedezics
				}
			}
			every_owned_pop = {
				limit = {
					is_same_species = event_target:arcticezics
				}
				change_species = event_target:infusedezics
			}
			while = { count = 5		create_army = { name = "Infused Ezicanias Legions"	owner = event_target:flusion_primitives_country species = event_target:infusedezics type = "flusion_army" } }
		}
	}
	option = { name = "giga_psychic_beacon.00611.a" }
}

# Planet Imprisoned
country_event = {
	id = giga_psychic_beacon.007
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		ehof_default_country = yes
		NOR = {
			has_technology = giga_tech_psychic_beacon
			is_researching_technology = giga_tech_psychic_beacon
			has_tech_option = giga_tech_psychic_beacon
		}
		has_technology = tech_mega_engineering
		any_owned_leader = {
			OR = {
				has_trait = leader_trait_admiral_chosen
				has_trait = leader_trait_general_chosen
				has_trait = leader_trait_governor_chosen
				has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
				has_trait = leader_trait_scientist_chosen
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			90 = {
				modifier = { add = -5 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 1 } }
				modifier = { add = -10 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 2 } }
				modifier = { add = -15 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 3 } }
				modifier = { add = -20 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 4 } }
				modifier = { add = -25 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 5 } }
				modifier = { add = -30 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 6 } }
				modifier = { add = -35 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 7 } }
				modifier = { add = -40 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 8 } }
				modifier = { add = -45 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 9 } }
				modifier = { add = -50 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 10 } }
				modifier = { add = -55 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 11 } }
				modifier = { add = -60 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 12 } }
				modifier = { add = -65 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 13 } }
				modifier = { add = -70 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 14 } }
				modifier = { add = -75 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 15 } }
				modifier = { add = -80 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 16 } }
				modifier = { add = -85 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 17 } }
				modifier = { add = -90 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value >= 18 } }
				modifier = { factor = 0 has_country_flag = has_shroud_patron }
				change_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 1 }
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = { add = 5 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 1 } }
				modifier = { add = 10 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 2 } }
				modifier = { add = 15 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 3 } }
				modifier = { add = 20 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 4 } }
				modifier = { add = 25 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 5 } }
				modifier = { add = 30 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 6 } }
				modifier = { add = 35 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 7 } }
				modifier = { add = 40 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 8 } }
				modifier = { add = 45 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 9 } }
				modifier = { add = 50 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 10 } }
				modifier = { add = 55 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 11 } }
				modifier = { add = 60 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 12 } }
				modifier = { add = 65 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 13 } }
				modifier = { add = 70 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 14 } }
				modifier = { add = 75 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 15 } }
				modifier = { add = 80 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 16 } }
				modifier = { add = 85 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 17 } }
				modifier = { add = 90 check_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value >= 18 } }
				modifier = { factor = 10 has_country_flag = has_shroud_patron }
				set_variable = { which = giga_psionic_beacon_tech value = 0 }
				country_event = { id = giga_psychic_beacon.008 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = giga_psychic_beacon.008
	title = "utopia.3000.name"
	desc = "giga_psychic_beacon.008.desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	diplomatic_title = BLANK_STRING
	force_open = yes
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = shroud1
		room = shroud_room
	}

	immediate = { set_country_flag = shroud_diplomacy_engaged }
	after = { hidden_effect = { remove_country_flag = shroud_diplomacy_engaged } }

	option = {
		name = "giga_psychic_beacon.008.a"
		add_research_option = giga_tech_psychic_beacon
		add_tech_progress = { tech = giga_tech_psychic_beacon progress = 0.1 }
	}
}

# Conjure
country_event = {
	id = giga_psychic_beacon.010
	title = "giga_psychic_beacon.010.name"
	desc = "giga_psychic_beacon.010.desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal

	diplomatic = yes

	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = shroud1
		room = shroud_room
	}

	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { exists = event_target:giga_planet_picker_001 } clear_global_event_target = giga_planet_picker_001 }
		if = { limit = { exists = event_target:giga_planet_picker_002 } clear_global_event_target = giga_planet_picker_002 }
		if = { limit = { exists = event_target:giga_planet_picker_003 } clear_global_event_target = giga_planet_picker_003 }
		if = { limit = { exists = event_target:giga_planet_picker_004 } clear_global_event_target = giga_planet_picker_004 }
		if = { limit = { exists = event_target:giga_planet_picker_005 } clear_global_event_target = giga_planet_picker_005 }
		if = { limit = { exists = event_target:giga_planet_picker_006 } clear_global_event_target = giga_planet_picker_006 }

# Planet Conjured
country_event = {
	id = giga_psychic_beacon.011
	title = "giga_psychic_beacon.011.name"
	desc = "giga_psychic_beacon.011.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_zro_3
	location = event_target:giga_planet_illuminated
	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal_light
	option = { name = "giga_psychic_beacon.011.a" }
}

# Armies done
country_event = {
	id = giga_psychic_beacon.0111
	title = "giga_psychic_beacon.0111.name"
	desc = "giga_psychic_beacon.0111.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_zro_3
	location = event_target:giga_planet_illuminated
	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal_light

	trigger = {
		from = {
			NOT = { is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium }
		}
		fromfrom = {
			has_planet_flag = beacon_armies_conjured
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_owned_army = {
			limit = {
				army_type = beacon_shroud_army_defensive
				NOT = {
					planet = {
						any_planet_army = { owner = { is_at_war_with = ROOT } }
					}
				}
			}
			remove_army = yes
		}
		fromfrom = { remove_planet_flag = beacon_armies_conjured }
	}

	option = {
		name = "giga_psychic_beacon.0111.a" 
		custom_tooltip = "giga_psychic_beacon.0111.a.tooltip" 
	}
}

# Invasion Failed
country_event = {
	id = giga_psychic_beacon.0112
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		from = {
			NOT = { is_country_type = katzenartig_imperium }
		}
		fromfrom = {
			has_planet_flag = beacon_armies_conjured
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		fromfrom = { remove_planet_flag = beacon_armies_conjured }
	}
}

# Imprint Failed
country_event = {
	id = giga_psychic_beacon.0151
	title = "giga_psychic_beacon.0151.name"
	desc = "giga_psychic_beacon.0151.desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_sound = event_bad_omen
	picture = GFX_evt_unspeakable_horror

	option = {
		name = "giga_psychic_beacon.0151.a"
		custom_tooltip = "giga_psychic_beacon.0151.a.tooltip"
		hidden_effect = {
			refund_residue = yes
			event_target:giga_leader_imprinted = {
				kill_leader = {
					show_notification = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Imprint succesful
country_event = {
	id = giga_psychic_beacon.0152
	title = "giga_psychic_beacon.0152.name"
	desc = "giga_psychic_beacon.0152.desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal_light
	picture = GFX_evt_zro_3
	
	option = {
		name = "giga_psychic_beacon.0152.a"
		custom_tooltip = "giga_psychic_beacon.0152.a.tooltip"
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:giga_leader_imprinted = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_trait = leader_trait_admiral_psionic }
					}
					add_trait = leader_trait_admiral_psionic
				}
				random_list = {
					30 = {
						add_trait = leader_trait_admiral_astute
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_trait = leader_trait_admiral_astute
						}
					}
					30 = {
						add_trait = leader_trait_admiral_fortifier
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_trait = leader_trait_admiral_fortifier
						}
					}
					30 = {
						add_trait = leader_trait_admiral_farsighted
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_trait = leader_trait_admiral_farsighted
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Sublimate on purge
planet_event = {
	id = giga_psychic_beacon.999
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		from = {
			has_technology = giga_tech_psychic_beacon
			any_owned_megastructure = {
				OR = {
					is_megastructure_type = psychic_beacon_3
					is_megastructure_type = psychic_beacon_4
				}
			}
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			is_robot_pop = no
			has_job = purge_psionic_sublimation
		}
		is_controlled_by = FROM
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROM = { NOT = { has_trait = trait_psionic } }
			}
			FROM = { add_resource = { sr_psionic_sublimate = 2 } }
		}
		else = {
			FROM = { add_resource = { sr_psionic_sublimate = 10 } }
		}
	}
}
